NV_BASIC#
Basic Skill
Max Level: 9
Skill Form: ^6666CCPassive^000000
Description: ^777777Enables the use of Basic
Interface Skills.^000000
[Lv 1]: Enables Trading
^777777You can trade ^990099Item^777777 and ^990099Zeny^777777 with other
^00A100Player^777777.
^990000Right click on a player to initiate.^000000
[Lv 2]: Enables Emotions
^777777Alt+(0~9) and Ctrl+(1,-,=.)
Alt+L will open ^990099Emoticon Window^777777.^000000
[Lv 3]: Enables Sitting
^777777Doubles HP and SP regen speed.
^990000Press the Insert key or type /sit.^000000
[Lv 4]: Enables Chat Room Creation
^777777Alt+C to open a Chat Room.^000000
[Lv 5]: Joins a Party
^777777Character can join a party.^000000
[Lv 6]: Enables Use of Kafra Storage
^777777Talk to ^0000FFKafra Staff^777777 to open ^990099Storage^777777.^000000
[Lv 7]: Organize a Party
^777777Creates a party
Type ^990099/organize "Party Name"^777777
Set party options in the Party Window (Alt+Z).^000000
[Lv 9]: Enables Change to First Job Class
^777777Qualifies character for change from
^00A100Novice^777777 to one of the ^00A100First^777777 or ^00A100Expanded^777777
classes.^000000

If you ^0000FFClimax^777777 status active,
the effect will change according to
the ^0000FFClimax^777777 skill level:
^8041D9Level 1 Climax^777777: Decreases the spawn interval
of the flower buds by half.
^CC723DLevel 2 Climax^777777: Explodes twice as many flowers.
^47C83ELevel 3 Climax^777777: Increases damage
of ^0000FFAll Bloom^777777 by 300%.
^4641D9Level 4 Climax^777777: ^0000FFAll Bloom^777777
will not inflict damage, but all targets
within range will receive increased ^FF0000Fire^777777
elemental damage by 100% for 30 seconds.
^CC3D3DLevel 5 Climax^777777: Upon all flower buds exploded,
inflict 85000% ^FF0000Fire^777777 elemantal magic damage to
all targets within flower garden.^000000
